								event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
									change_variable = {
										which = "katzen_douclaw_current_system_count"
										value = 1
									}
								}
							}
						}
						create_katzen_douclaw = yes
					}
				}
				count_katzen_planets_and_systems = yes #ATTEMPT TO SPAWN LORIS IF HE'S NOT DEAD, HE GETS ANOTHER 40%
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = loris_removed }
						check_variable = { #More than 4 systems left, loris can spawn
							which = "katzen_total_system_count"
							value > 4
						}
						check_variable = { #More than 2 planets left, loris can spawn
							which = "katzen_total_planet_count"
							value > 0
						}
					}
					random_planet_within_border = { #designate one planet as the capital
						limit = {
							owner = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium }
							solar_system = {
								NOT = { has_star_flag = flusion_system }
							}
							is_colony = yes
						}
						save_global_event_target_as = katzen_loris_capital
						solar_system = { set_star_flag = katzen_loris_system }
						count_katzen_planets_and_systems = yes
						event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
							set_variable = {
								which = "katzen_loris_system_count"
								value = 0
							}
							set_variable = {
								which = "katzen_loris_system_count"
								value = "katzen_total_system_count"
							}
							if = {
								limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = loris_removed } }
								divide_variable = {
									which = "katzen_loris_system_count"
									value = 2.5
								}
							}
							else = {
								divide_variable = {
									which = "katzen_loris_system_count"
									value = 1.67
								}
							}
							round_variable = katzen_loris_system_count
							set_variable = {
								which = "katzen_loris_current_system_count"
								value = 0
							}
						}
						while = {
							limit = { #stop when current loris systems surpass 25% of katzen systems
								event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
									check_variable = {
										which = "katzen_loris_current_system_count"
										value < katzen_loris_system_count
									}
								}
							}
							every_system = { #claim all neighbor systems
								limit = { has_star_flag = katzen_loris_system }
								every_neighbor_system = {
									limit = {
										owner = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium }
										NOR = {
											has_star_flag = flusion_system
											has_star_flag = katzen_loris_system
										}
									}
									set_star_flag = katzen_loris_system
								}
							}
							event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
								set_variable = {
									which = "katzen_loris_current_system_count"
									value = 0
								}
							}
							every_system = { #count current loris systems
								limit = { has_star_flag = katzen_loris_system }
								event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
									change_variable = {
										which = "katzen_loris_current_system_count"
										value = 1
									}
								}
							}
						}
						create_katzen_loris = yes
					}
				}
				count_katzen_planets_and_systems = yes #ATTEMPT TO SPAWN DIETRICH, HE GETS 12% AND 40% IF LORIS IS DEAD
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { #More than 4 systems left, dietrich can spawn
							which = "katzen_total_system_count"
							value > 4
						}
						check_variable = { #More than 2 planets left, dietrich can spawn
							which = "katzen_total_planet_count"
							value > 0
						}
					}
					random_planet_within_border = { #designate one planet as the capital
						limit = {
							owner = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium }
							solar_system = {
								NOT = { has_star_flag = flusion_system }
							}
							is_colony = yes
						}
						save_global_event_target_as = katzen_dietrich_capital
						solar_system = { set_star_flag = katzen_dietrich_system }
						count_katzen_planets_and_systems = yes
						event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
							set_variable = {
								which = "katzen_dietrich_system_count"
								value = 0
							}
							set_variable = {
								which = "katzen_dietrich_system_count"
								value = "katzen_total_system_count"
							}
							if = { #Douclaw is there, Loris isn't dead
								limit = { 
									NOT = { has_global_flag = loris_removed } 
									has_global_flag = giga_douclaw_stayed_behind
								}
								divide_variable = {
									which = "katzen_dietrich_system_count"
									value = 8
								}
							}
							else_if = { #Douclaw is there, Loris is dead
								limit = { 
									has_global_flag = loris_removed 
									has_global_flag = giga_douclaw_stayed_behind
								}
								divide_variable = {
									which = "katzen_dietrich_system_count"
									value = 2.5
								}
							}
							else_if = { #Douclaw left, Loris is dead
								limit = { 
									has_global_flag = loris_removed 
									NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_douclaw_stayed_behind }
								}
								divide_variable = {
									which = "katzen_dietrich_system_count"
									value = 1.2
								}
								set_global_flag = giga_big_dietrich
							}
							round_variable = katzen_dietrich_system_count
							set_variable = {
								which = "katzen_dietrich_current_system_count"
								value = 0
							}
						}
						while = {
							limit = { #stop when current dietrich systems surpass 25% of katzen systems
								event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
									check_variable = {
										which = "katzen_dietrich_current_system_count"
										value < katzen_dietrich_system_count
									}
								}
							}
							every_system = { #claim all neighbor systems
								limit = { has_star_flag = katzen_dietrich_system }
								every_neighbor_system = {
									limit = {
										owner = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium }
										NOR = {
											has_star_flag = flusion_system
											has_star_flag = katzen_dietrich_system
										}
									}
									set_star_flag = katzen_dietrich_system
								}
							}
							event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
								set_variable = {
									which = "katzen_dietrich_current_system_count"
									value = 0
								}
							}
							every_system = { #count current dietrich systems
								limit = { has_star_flag = katzen_dietrich_system }
								event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
									change_variable = {
										which = "katzen_dietrich_current_system_count"
										value = 1
									}
								}
							}
						}
						create_katzen_dietrich = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
			every_system_within_border = {
				limit = {
					any_system_planet = {
						is_colony = yes
						owner = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium }
					}
					NOR = {
						has_star_flag = flusion_system
						has_star_flag = solakian_system
						has_star_flag = laurandar_system
						has_star_flag = kronk_system
						has_star_flag = katzen_socialist_system
						has_star_flag = katzen_realm_system
						has_star_flag = katzen_junta_system
						has_star_flag = katzen_republic_system
					}
				}
				random_system_planet = {
					limit = {
						is_colony = yes
						owner = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium }
					}
					create_katzen_splinter_state = yes
				}
			}
		}
		every_megastructure = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_megastructure_type = katzen_forge_0
					is_megastructure_type = katzen_forge_1
				}
			}
			remove_megastructure = THIS
		}
		every_system = {
			every_fleet_in_system = {
				limit = { has_fleet_flag = warforge_platform }
				destroy_fleet = THIS
			}
			every_fleet_in_system = {
				limit = { has_fleet_flag = katzen_planet_platform }
				destroy_fleet = THIS
			}
		}
		event_target:giga_jublio_system = {
			every_system_planet = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
					}
				}
				set_owner = solar_system.space_owner
			}
		}
		every_system = {
			limit = { has_star_flag = solakian_system }
			remove_star_flag = solakian_system
		}
		every_system = {
			limit = { has_star_flag = laurandar_system }
			remove_star_flag = laurandar_system
		}
		every_system = {
			limit = { has_star_flag = kronk_system }
			remove_star_flag = kronk_system
		}
		every_galaxy_planet = { #transfers planets in occupied land to controller
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
				}
				solar_system = {
					space_owner = {
						NOT = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium }
					}
				}
			}
			set_owner = solar_system.space_owner
		}
		destroy_country = yes #farewell
		event_target:flusion_conqueror = { #Achievement
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_achievements_disabled }
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1
					}
					NOR = {
						has_global_flag = katzenartig_deathwish
						has_global_flag = katzenartig_stellarite
						has_global_flag = katzenartig_improbable
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1_notification days = 30 }
				giga_achievement_sound = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_achievements_disabled }
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser2
					}
					has_global_flag = katzenartig_deathwish
				}
				set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1
				set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser2
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = giga_achievement_kaiser2_notification days = 30 }
				giga_achievement_sound = yes
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = beat_wildride_kaiser
					days = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_achievements_disabled }
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser3
					}
					has_global_flag = katzenartig_stellarite
				}
				set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1
				set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser2
				set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser3
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = giga_achievement_kaiser3_notification days = 30 }
				giga_achievement_sound = yes
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = beat_stellarite_kaiser
					days = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_achievements_disabled }
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser8
					}
					has_global_flag = katzenartig_improbable
				}
				set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1
				set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser2
				set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser3
				set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser8
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = giga_achievement_kaiser8_notification days = 30 }
				giga_achievement_sound = yes
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = beat_improbable_kaiser
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			country_event = { id = giga_katzen.097 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_modifier = solak_partisans_1 }
				remove_modifier = solak_partisans_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_modifier = solak_partisans_2 }
				remove_modifier = solak_partisans_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_modifier = solak_partisans_3 }
				remove_modifier = solak_partisans_3
			}
		}
		if = { #if flusion got blown up
			limit = {
				any_country = { has_country_flag = blew_up_flusion_crisis }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = blew_up_flusion_crisis }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1
						}
						NOR = {
							has_global_flag = katzenartig_deathwish
							has_global_flag = katzenartig_stellarite
							has_global_flag = katzenartig_improbable
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1
					set_timed_country_flag = { flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1_notification days = 30 }
					giga_achievement_sound = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser2
						}
						has_global_flag = katzenartig_deathwish
					}
					set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1
					set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser2
					set_timed_country_flag = { flag = giga_achievement_kaiser2_notification days = 30 }
					giga_achievement_sound = yes
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = beat_wildride_kaiser
						days = -1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser3
						}
						has_global_flag = katzenartig_stellarite
					}
					set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1
					set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser2
					set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser3
					set_timed_country_flag = { flag = giga_achievement_kaiser3_notification days = 30 }
					giga_achievement_sound = yes
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = beat_stellarite_kaiser
						days = -1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser8
						}
						has_global_flag = katzenartig_improbable
					}
					set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser1
					set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser2
					set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser3
					set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser8
					set_timed_country_flag = { flag = giga_achievement_kaiser8_notification days = 30 }
					giga_achievement_sound = yes
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = beat_improbable_kaiser
						days = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #they get angry if flusion got cracked (big surprise)
			limit = { has_global_flag = giga_player_country_cracked_flusion }
			event_target:player_country_cracked_flusion = { 
				country_event = { id = giga_flusionoperations.501 days = 40 }
			}
		}
		if = { #federation
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = giga_player_country_cracked_flusion
				AND = {
					exists = event_target:solakia
					event_target:solakia = { is_subject = no }
				}
				AND = {
					exists = event_target:laurandar
					event_target:laurandar = { is_subject = no }
				}
				AND = {
					exists = event_target:kronkcountry
					event_target:kronkcountry = { is_subject = no }
				}
			}
			event_target:player_country_cracked_flusion = { 
				country_event = { id = giga_flusionoperations.502 days = 120 }
			}
		}
		set_update_modifiers_batch = end
	}
}

country_event = { #Message about collapse
	id = giga_katzen.097
	title = "giga_katzen.097.name"
	desc = "giga_katzen.097.desc"

	picture = GFX_evt_partition
	show_sound = event_radio_chatter

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #huzzah!
		name = "giga_katzen.097.a"
	}
}

###PLANET DEVELOPMENT (non flusion)###
###CONQUERED WORLD EXPANSION####
planet_event = { #After a month
	id = giga_katzen.1001
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
		}
	}

	immediate = { #1 army
		set_update_modifiers_batch = begin
		rename_planet_katzen = yes
		while = { count = 1	create_army = { name = NAME_katzenarmee	owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country species = event_target:flusion_katzens type = "flusion_army" } }
		planet_event = { id = giga_katzen.102 days = 1800 random = 200 }
		katzen_clear_capitals = yes #remove old capital
		add_building = building_giga_katzen_capital
		create_pop = { #Pop in some Katzens
			species = event_target:flusion_katzens
			count = 2
		}
		create_pop = { #Sprinkle in some ezics
			species = event_target:arcticezics
		}
		create_pop = { #Sprinkle in some solakians
			species = event_target:solakians
		}
		event_target:flusion_primitives_country = { #Defensive platform
			create_fleet = {
				name = "Katzenplanetenverteidigung"
				settings = {
					spawn_debris = no
				}
				effect = {
					set_owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
					create_ship = {
						name = "Katzenplanetenverteidigung"
						design = "Meoder"
						upgradable = no
					}
					set_location = ROOT
					set_fleet_flag = katzen_planet_platform
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					is_planet_class = pc_habitat
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable
				}
			}
			add_district = district_city_katzen
			add_district = district_farming
			add_district = district_generator
			add_district = district_mining
			add_district = district_industrial
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			add_district = district_hab_housing
			add_district = district_hab_energy
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable }
			add_district = district_rw_city
			add_district = district_rw_farming
		}
		set_planet_flag = katzen_conquered_planet
		set_update_modifiers_batch = end
	}
}

planet_event = { #After 5 more years, add even more pops + take advantage of new districts
	id = giga_katzen.103
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_update_modifiers_batch = begin
		planet_event = { id = giga_katzen.104 days = 1800 random = 200 }
		create_pop = {
			species = event_target:flusion_katzens
			count = 3
		}
		create_pop = { #The other flusion species move in
			species = event_target:flusionians
			count = 2
		}
		create_pop = {
			species = event_target:solakians
		}
		create_pop = { #The other flusion species move in
			species = event_target:kronks
		}
		create_pop = { #Sprinkle in some ezics
			species = event_target:arcticezics
		}
		add_building = building_foundry_3 #Fun
		add_building = building_factory_3
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					is_planet_class = pc_habitat
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable
				}
			}
			add_district = district_city_katzen
			add_district = district_farming
			add_district = district_industrial
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			add_district = district_hab_housing
			add_district = district_hab_energy
			add_district = district_hab_energy
			# add_district = district_hab_cultural
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable }
			add_district = district_rw_science
		}
		set_update_modifiers_batch = end
	}
}

planet_event = { #After 5 more years, add even more pops + take advantage of new districts
	id = giga_katzen.104
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_update_modifiers_batch = begin
		create_pop = {
			species = event_target:flusion_katzens
			count = 3
		}
		create_pop = { #The other flusion species move in
			species = event_target:flusionians
			count = 2
		}
		create_pop = {
			species = event_target:solakians
		}
		create_pop = { #The other flusion species move in
			species = event_target:kronks
		}
		create_pop = { #Sprinkle in some ezics
			species = event_target:arcticezics
		}
		add_building = building_giga_flusion_fusion_power_plant #Fun
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					is_planet_class = pc_habitat
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable
				}
			}
			add_district = district_city_katzen
			add_district = district_farming
			add_district = district_industrial
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			add_district = district_hab_housing
			add_district = district_hab_energy
			add_district = district_hab_energy
			# add_district = district_hab_cultural
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable }
			add_district = district_rw_commercial
		}
		set_update_modifiers_batch = end
	}
}

###COLONIZED WORLD EXPANSION###
#The first event determines what to do with the world.
#If it is a planet the Katzens just colonized, do nothing.
#If it is a planet the Katzens conquered, determine its purpose.
#If it is a planet the Katzens REconquered, set it back to what it was.
planet_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.110

	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_update_modifiers_batch = begin
		set_controller = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
		set_owner =	event_target:flusion_primitives_country
		katzen_clear_capitals = yes
		add_building = building_giga_katzen_capital
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_set_up } }
			set_planet_flag = katzen_planet_set_up
			if = { #Conquered
				limit = { NOT = { has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_colonized } }
				while = { count = 1	create_army = { name = NAME_katzen_peacekeeper	owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country species = event_target:flusion_katzens type = "flusion_army" } }
			}
			if = { #Colonized
				limit = { has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_colonized }
				create_pop = { #Pop in some Katzens for good measure
					species = event_target:flusion_katzens
					count = 3
				}
				create_pop = {
					species = event_target:kronks
					count = 2
				}
				create_pop = {
					species = event_target:arcticezics
				}
				while = { count = 1	create_army = { name = NAME_katzencolonial_army	owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country species = event_target:flusion_katzens type = "flusion_army" } }
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					set_planet_flag = giga_katzen_forge_world
				}
				50 = {
					set_planet_flag = giga_katzen_research_world
				}
				0 = { #Siegfried World. All artificially terraformed planets surrounding Jublio will become Siegfried worlds, and terraformed planets themselves have a 40% chance of becoming one.
					set_planet_flag = giga_katzen_fortress_world
					modifier = {
						add = 50 #CHANGE
						has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_colonized
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 200
						has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_colonized
						solar_system = { has_star_flag = flusion_system }
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 200
						has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_colonized
						solar_system = { any_neighbor_system = { has_star_flag = flusion_system } }
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 200
						has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_colonized
						solar_system = { any_neighbor_system = { any_neighbor_system = { has_star_flag = flusion_system } } }
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 200
						has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_colonized
						solar_system = { any_neighbor_system = { any_neighbor_system = { any_neighbor_system = { has_star_flag = flusion_system } } } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						solar_system = { any_system_planet = { has_planet_flag = giga_katzen_fortress_world } }
					}
				}
			}
			planet_event = { id = giga_katzen.111 days = 60 }
		}
		else = { #Reconquered
			while = { count = 1	create_army = { name = NAME_katzen_peacekeeper	owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country species = event_target:flusion_katzens type = "flusion_army" } }
			event_target:flusion_primitives_country = { #Make a defensive platform
				create_fleet = {
					name = "Katzenplanetenverteidigung"
					settings = { spawn_debris = no }
					effect = {
						set_owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
						create_ship = {
							name = "Katzenplanetenverteidigung"
							design = "Meoder"
							upgradable = no
						}
						set_location = {
							target = ROOT
							distance = 0
							angle = 0
						}
						set_fleet_flag = katzen_planet_platform
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_update_modifiers_batch = end
	}
}

#After 2 months, run a check.
#If it is conquered and has less than 15 pops, move it all to Flusion.
#Else, spawn another army and put a defence platform.
planet_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.111
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_update_modifiers_batch = begin
		if = { #Empty it if not enough pops
			limit = {
				OR = {
					count_owned_pop = { count < 11 }
					planet_size < 9 #Not worth the Kaiser's time if it's that small
				}
				solar_system = { NOT = { has_star_flag = flusion_system } }
				NOT = { has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_colonized }
			}
			every_owned_pop = {
				resettle_pop = {
					pop = THIS
					planet = event_target:gigaflusion
				}
			}
			remove_planet_flag = katzen_planet_set_up
			if = { 
				limit = { has_planet_flag = giga_katzen_fortress_world }
				remove_planet_flag = giga_katzen_fortress_world
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { has_planet_flag = giga_katzen_forge_world }
				remove_planet_flag = giga_katzen_forge_world
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { has_planet_flag = giga_katzen_research_world }
				remove_planet_flag = giga_katzen_research_world
			}
			destroy_colony = yes
		}
		else = {
			if = { #Rename now
				limit = { solar_system = { NOT = { has_star_flag = flusion_system } } }
				rename_planet_katzen = yes
			}
			if = { #If the planet was conquered, add Katzens & Army
				limit = { NOT = { has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_colonized } }
				while = { count = 1	create_army = { name = NAME_katzen_peacekeeper	owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country species = event_target:flusion_katzens type = "flusion_army" } }
				create_pop = { 
					species = event_target:flusion_katzens 
					count = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_colonized }
				add_building = building_giga_katzen_terraformer #The terraformer
			}
			event_target:flusion_primitives_country = { #Make a defensive platform
				create_fleet = {
					name = "Katzenplanetenverteidigung"
					settings = { spawn_debris = no }
					effect = {
						set_owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
						create_ship = {
							name = "Katzenplanetenverteidigung"
							design = "Meoder"
							upgradable = no
						}
						set_location = {
							target = ROOT
							distance = 0
							angle = 0
						}
						set_fleet_flag = katzen_planet_platform
					}
				}
			} 
			#Add some districts
			add_district = district_city_katzen
			add_district = district_city_katzen
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_planet_flag = giga_katzen_forge_world
					has_planet_flag = giga_katzen_research_world
				}
				NOR = {
					habitable_structure = yes
					planet_size > 30
				}
			}
			planet_event = { id = giga_katzen.112 days = 1080 } #expand again
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_planet_flag = giga_katzen_fortress_world
			}
			planet_event = { id = giga_katzen.1121 days = 1080 }
		}
		# if = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		NOR = {
		# 			is_planet_class = pc_habitat
		# 			is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# 	add_district = district_generator
		# 	add_district = district_mining
		# 	add_district = district_industrial
		# }
		# else_if = {
		# 	limit = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		# 	add_district = district_hab_housing
		# 	add_district = district_hab_commercial
		# 	add_district = district_hab_cultural
		# }
		# else_if = {
		# 	limit = { is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable }
		# 	add_district = district_rw_city
		# 	add_district = district_rw_farming
		# }
		set_update_modifiers_batch = end
	}
}

planet_event = { #After 3 years, begin developping it based on specialization
	id = giga_katzen.112
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_planet_flag = giga_katzen_planet_specialized } }
			set_planet_flag = giga_katzen_planet_specialized
		}
		clear_blockers = yes
		remove_all_buildings = yes
		remove_all_districts = yes
		add_building = building_giga_katzen_capital
		if = {
			limit = { has_planet_flag = katzen_planet_colonized }
			create_pop = { species = event_target:solakians }
			create_pop = { species = event_target:kronks }
			create_pop = { species = event_target:arcticezics }
			create_pop = { species = event_target:flusion_katzens }
		}
		create_pop = { species = event_target:solakians }
		create_pop = { species = event_target:kronks }
		create_pop = { species = event_target:arcticezics }
		create_pop = { species = event_target:flusion_katzens }

		#How could I forget? The Flusion tax! 10% of pops go to Flusion (best planet)
		every_owned_pop = {
			random_list = {
				90 = {}
				10 = {
					resettle_pop = {
						pop = THIS
						planet = event_target:gigaflusion
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						event_target:gigaflusion = {
							has_planet_flag = flusion_fully_built_up
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		#It is time for math.
		#The amount of pops allowed to be on a Katzen planet that is not Flusion is equal to thrice the size of the planet.
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_katzen_planet_max_num_pops
			value = 0
		}
		export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
			trigger = planet_size
			variable = giga_katzen_planet_max_num_pops
		}
		multiply_variable = { #This is the max number of pops.
			which = giga_katzen_planet_max_num_pops
			value = 3
		}

		set_variable = {
			which = giga_katzen_planet_num_pops
			value = 0
		}
		export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
			trigger = num_pops
			variable = giga_katzen_planet_num_pops
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = giga_katzen_planet_num_pops
					value > giga_katzen_planet_max_num_pops
				}
				event_target:gigaflusion = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = flusion_fully_built_up }
				}
			}
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = giga_katzen_planet_num_pops value > giga_katzen_planet_max_num_pops } }
				random_owned_pop = {
					resettle_pop = {
						pop = THIS
						planet = event_target:gigaflusion
					}
				}
				export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
					trigger = num_pops
					variable = giga_katzen_planet_num_pops
				}
			}
		}
		#A Katzen planet is considered "built up" to the max if its pop is equal to thrice its planet size.
		#Now we know there's going to be enough housing.
		#Each housing district provides 6 housing, thus we need to fill half the planet with housing to ensure no overcrowding
		export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
			trigger = free_district_slots
			variable = giga_katzen_district_slots
		}
		divide_variable = {
			which = giga_katzen_district_slots
			value = 2
		}
		ceiling_variable = giga_katzen_district_slots
		while = {
			count = giga_katzen_district_slots
			add_district = district_city_katzen
		}
		add_building = building_planetary_shield_generator #Shield
		#Each theater provides 24 amenities, so we need (Max pops)/24 buildings
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_katzen_theater_count
			value = giga_katzen_planet_max_num_pops
		}
		divide_variable = {
			which = giga_katzen_theater_count
			value = 40
		}
		floor_variable = giga_katzen_theater_count
		while = {
			count = giga_katzen_theater_count
			add_building = building_katzen_theater
		}
		add_building = building_katzen_theater
		#Now that amenities are solved, we just fill the rest with enough foundries to accodomate the population.
		if = {
			limit = { has_planet_flag = giga_katzen_forge_world }
			export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
				trigger = free_building_slots
				variable = giga_katzen_building_slots
			}
			export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
				trigger = num_pops
				variable = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
			}
			divide_variable = {
				which = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
				value = 8
			}
			ceiling_variable = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
			if = { #If more to be built than build slots, equalize
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
						value > giga_katzen_building_slots
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
					value = giga_katzen_building_slots
				}
			}
			while = {
				count = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
				add_building = building_katzen_foundry
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_planet_flag = giga_katzen_research_world }
			export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
				trigger = free_building_slots
				variable = giga_katzen_building_slots
			}
			export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
				trigger = num_pops
				variable = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
			}
			divide_variable = {
				which = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
				value = 8
			}
			ceiling_variable = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
			if = { #If more to be built than build slots, equalize
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
						value > giga_katzen_building_slots
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
					value = giga_katzen_building_slots
				}
			}
			while = {
				count = giga_katzen_planet_foundry_count
				add_building = building_katzen_science
			}
		}
		while = { count = 2	create_army = { name = NAME_katzen_garrison	owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country species = event_target:flusion_katzens type = "flusion_army" } }
		#Add 1 of each basic district
		# add_district = district_generator
		# add_district = district_mining
		# add_district = district_farming
		#If there is STILL unemployment, start adding basic districts
		# if = {
		# 	limit = { num_unemployed > 1 }
		# 	export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
		# 		trigger = num_unemployed
		# 		variable = giga_katzen_extra_district_count_unemployed
		# 	}
		# 	divide_variable = {
		# 		which = giga_katzen_extra_district_count_unemployed
		# 		value = 2
		# 	}
		# 	ceiling_variable = giga_katzen_extra_district_count_unemployed
		# 	export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
		# 		trigger = free_district_slots
		# 		variable = giga_katzen_district_slots
		# 	}
		# 	if = {
		# 		limit = { #equalize if more districts than possible
		# 			check_variable = {
		# 				which = giga_katzen_extra_district_count_unemployed
		# 				value > giga_katzen_district_slots
		# 			}
		# 		}
		# 		set_variable = {
		# 			which = giga_katzen_extra_district_count_unemployed
		# 			value = giga_katzen_district_slots
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# 	while = {
		# 		count = giga_katzen_extra_district_count_unemployed
		# 		random_list = {
		# 			10 = { add_district = district_generator }
		# 			10 = { add_district = district_farming }
		# 			10 = { add_district = district_mining }
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# }
	}
}

#Develop Siegfried World
planet_event = { #After 3 years, add fortresses (fun times)
	id = giga_katzen.1121
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		planet_event = { id = giga_katzen.1131 days = 1800 random = 200 } #CHANGE MORE
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_planet_flag = giga_katzen_planet_specialized } }
			set_planet_flag = giga_katzen_planet_specialized
		}
		clear_blockers = yes
		remove_all_buildings = yes
		remove_all_districts = yes
		add_building = building_giga_katzen_capital
		#8 Katzens
		create_pop = { 
			species = event_target:flusion_katzens
			count = 8 
		}

		#How could I forget? The Flusion tax! 10% of pops go to Flusion (best planet)
		every_owned_pop = {
			random_list = {
				90 = {}
				10 = {
					resettle_pop = {
						pop = THIS
						planet = event_target:gigaflusion
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						event_target:gigaflusion = {
							NOT = { has_planet_flag = flusion_fully_built_up }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#A Katzen planet is considered "built up" to the max if its pop is equal to thrice its planet size.
		#Now we know there's going to be enough housing.
		#Each housing district provides 6 housing, thus we need to fill half the planet with housing to ensure no overcrowding
		export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
			trigger = free_district_slots
			variable = giga_katzen_district_slots
		}
		divide_variable = {
			which = giga_katzen_district_slots
			value = 2
		}
		ceiling_variable = giga_katzen_district_slots
		while = {
			count = giga_katzen_district_slots
			add_district = district_city_katzen
		}
		add_building = building_planetary_shield_generator #Shield
		#Add 1 of each basic district
		add_district = district_generator
		add_district = district_mining
		add_district = district_farming
		add_building = building_katzen_theater
		#Now that amenities are solved, we just fill the rest with enough foundries to accodomate the population.
		add_building = building_fortress
		add_building = building_fortress
		while = { count = 2	create_army = { name = NAME_katzen_garrison	owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country species = event_target:flusion_katzens type = "flusion_army" } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_planet_flag = siegfried_world}
			}
			set_planet_flag = siegfried_world
		}
		solar_system.starbase = { #Lvl 1
			set_starbase_size = starbase_starport
			set_starbase_module = {
				slot = 1
				module = detection_array
			}
			set_starbase_module = {
				slot = 2
				module = detection_array
			}
			fleet = {
				remove_modifier = warforge_detection
			}
		}
	}
}

planet_event = { #After 5 more years, turn it into a real siegfried world (do not hang the washing on it please)
	id = giga_katzen.1131
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		#2 Katzens
		create_pop = { 
			species = event_target:flusion_katzens 
			count = 2
		}
		
		add_building = building_fortress

		#How could I forget? The Flusion tax! 10% of pops go to Flusion (best planet)
		every_owned_pop = {
			random_list = {
				90 = {}
				10 = {
					resettle_pop = {
						pop = THIS
						planet = event_target:gigaflusion
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						event_target:gigaflusion = {
							NOT = { has_planet_flag = flusion_fully_built_up }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		change_pc = {
			class = pc_giga_siegfried_world
			inherit_entity = yes
		}
		
		solar_system = {
			set_star_flag = siegfried_anti_jump_star
			every_neighbor_system = { set_star_flag = siegfried_anti_jump_star }
		}

		add_building = building_giga_siegfried_global_bunker

		create_fleet = { #Siegfried defenses
			name = "Siegfried Array"
			settings = {
				spawn_debris = no
			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
				create_ship = {
					name = "Katzenplanetenverteidigung"
					design = "Meoder"
					upgradable = no
				}
				set_location = {
					target = ROOT
					distance = 15
					angle = 0
				}
				set_fleet_flag = katzen_planet_platform
			}
		}

		create_fleet = { #Siegfried defenses
			name = "Siegfried Array"
			settings = {
				spawn_debris = no
			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
				create_ship = {

					design = "Meoder"

				}
				set_location = {
					target = ROOT
					distance = 15
					angle = 90
				}
				set_fleet_flag = katzen_planet_platform
			}
		}

		create_fleet = { #Siegfried defenses

					angle = 180
				}
				set_fleet_flag = katzen_planet_platform
			}
		}

		create_fleet = { #Siegfried defenses
			name = "Siegfried Array"
			settings = {

			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
				create_ship = {

				}
				set_location = {

				}
				set_fleet_flag = katzen_planet_platform
			}
		}

		while = { count = 4	create_army = { name = NAME_katzen_garrison	owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country species = event_target:flusion_katzens type = "flusion_army" } }
		planet_event = { id = giga_katzen.120 days = 10 }
		solar_system.starbase = { #Lvl 2
			set_starbase_size = starbase_starfortress
			set_starbase_module = {
				slot = 1
				module = detection_array
			}
			set_starbase_module = {
				slot = 2
				module = detection_array
			}
			set_starbase_module = {
				slot = 3
				module = detection_array
			}
			set_starbase_module = {
				slot = 4
				module = detection_array
			}
			set_starbase_module = {
				slot = 5
				module = detection_array
			}
			set_starbase_building = {
				slot = 1
				building = listening_post
			}
			set_starbase_building = {
				slot = 2
				building = communications_jammer
			}
			fleet = {
				remove_modifier = warforge_detection
			}
		}
	}
}

planet_event = { #After 5 more years, add even more pops + take advantage of new districts
	id = giga_katzen.113
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		planet_event = { id = giga_katzen.114 days = 1800 random = 200 }
		grow_katzen_colony = yes
		while = { count = 1	create_army = { name = NAME_katzen_panzers	owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country species = event_target:flusion_primitives_country type = "riesigerkatzenpanzer_defence" } }
		add_building = building_giga_flusion_fusion_power_plant
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					is_planet_class = pc_habitat
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable
				}
			}
			add_district = district_city_katzen
			add_district = district_farming
			add_district = district_farming
			add_district = district_generator
			add_district = district_generator
			add_district = district_industrial
			add_district = district_industrial
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			add_district = district_hab_housing
			add_district = district_hab_energy
			add_district = district_hab_energy
			# add_district = district_hab_cultural
		}
	}
}

#Siegfried world monthly check (they blow up if captured)
planet_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.120
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					owner = { NOT = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium } }
					is_colony = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_colony = yes }
				save_event_target_as = destroyed_siegfried_world
				owner = { country_event = { id = giga_katzen.121 } }
				destroy_colony = yes
			}
			remove_all_buildings = yes
			remove_all_districts = yes
			change_pc = pc_katzenland
			set_planet_entity = {
				entity = katzenland_01_entity
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = "irradiated_desert_planet"
				days = -1
			}
			while = {
				count = 12
				create_katzenland_deposits = yes
			}
			solar_system = {
				remove_star_flag = siegfried_anti_jump_star
				every_neighbor_system = { remove_star_flag = siegfried_anti_jump_star }
			}
		}
		else = {
			planet_event = { id = giga_katzen.120 days = 30 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.121
	title = "giga_katzen.121.name"
	desc = "giga_katzen.121.desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_evt_exploding_planet
	show_sound = event_super_explosion
	location = event_target:destroyed_siegfried_world


	option = { #NOOOO
		name = "giga_katzen.121.a"
		custom_tooltip = "giga_katzen.121.a.tooltip"
	}
}

#Siegfried Worlds blow up
country_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.123
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		every_galaxy_planet = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_giga_siegfried_world }
			if = {
				limit = { is_colony = yes }
				destroy_colony = yes
			}
			remove_all_buildings = yes
			remove_all_districts = yes
			change_pc = pc_katzenland
			set_planet_entity = {
				entity = katzenland_01_entity
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = "irradiated_desert_planet"
				days = -1
			}
			while = {
				count = 12
				create_katzenland_deposits = yes
			}
			solar_system = {
				remove_star_flag = siegfried_anti_jump_star
				every_neighbor_system = { remove_star_flag = siegfried_anti_jump_star }
			}
		}
		every_playable_country = {
			country_event = { id = giga_katzen.122 } 
		}
	}
}

#SUBMARINES
#destroyed if not katzen
ship_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.85000

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		is_ship_size = giga_katzen_submarine
		owner = { NOT = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium } }
	}

	immediate = {
		destroy_ship = ROOT
	}
}


ship_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.8500

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		is_ship_size = giga_katzen_submarine
		owner = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium }
	}

	immediate = {
		event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
			country_event = { id = giga_katzen.8501 days = 90 } #respawn at flusion 3 months later
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = set_katzen_submarine_variable } }
			set_global_flag = set_katzen_submarine_variable
			event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
				set_variable = {
					which = katzen_submarines_escaped
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = {
				event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
					change_variable = {
						which = katzen_submarines_escaped
						value = 1
					}
				}
				ROOT.solar_system = {
					create_ambient_object = {
						type = katzen_submarine_getaway_object
						location = ROOT
						duration = 5
						use_3d_location = yes
						entity_offset = 0
						scale = 1
					}
				}
				delete_ship = ROOT
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					ROOT.solar_system = {
						exists = starbase
						starbase = { has_starbase_building = katzen_submarine_snare }
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					ROOT.solar_system = {
						any_system_planet = {
							OR = {
								is_planet_class = pc_giga_maginot_world
								is_planet_class = pc_giga_maginot_gas_giant
								has_modifier = maginot_anti_jump_star_modifier
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			40 = {
				destroy_ship = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT.from.controller = { has_country_flag = blowing_up_katzen_subs } }
					ROOT.from.controller = {
						change_variable = {
							which = katzen_subs_destroyed
							value = 1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									which = katzen_subs_destroyed
									value = 15
								}
							}
							country_event = { id = giga_katzen.8511 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.8501

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
				NOT = { has_global_flag = katzenartig_imperium_defeated }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = katzen_submarines_escaped
						value >= 6
					}
				}
				subtract_variable = {
					which = katzen_submarines_escaped
					value = 6
				}
				country_event = { id = giga_katzen.8501 days = 5 }
				create_leader = {
					class = commander
					species = event_target:flusion_katzens
					name = random
					skill = 4
					traits = {
						trait = leader_trait_cautious
					}
					effect = {
						save_event_target_as = katzen_admiral
					}
				}
				create_fleet = { #Spawn a simple task force of bombers
					name = "Unterraumboot Force"
					settings = {
						spawn_debris = no
						can_upgrade = no
						uses_naval_capacity = no
						can_change_composition = no
					}
					effect = {
						set_owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
						while = {
							count = 6
							create_ship = {
								name = random
								design = "Kimitz"
								prefix = no
								effect = { set_disable_at_health = 0.05 set_name = "U-Boot" }
							}
						}
						assign_leader = event_target:katzen_admiral
						set_fleet_flag = katzen_reserve_fleet
						set_fleet_flag = katzen_submarine_fleet
						set_formation_scale = 2
						set_location = {
							target = event_target:gigaflusion
							distance = 50
							angle = random
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#large-scale deployment
country_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.8502

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	#5 years in the Katzens will deploy their submarines on a larger scale

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = katzenartig_imperium_defeated }
		exists = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = katzenartig_imperium_defeated }
				exists = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				country_event = { id = giga_katzen.8510 days = 10 }
			}
			set_global_flag = katzen_submarines_deployed
			set_country_flag = katzen_submarines_deployed
			create_leader = {
				class = commander
				species = event_target:flusion_katzens
				name = "Catser Von Kimitz"
				skill = 5
				gender = male
				traits = {
					trait = katzen_trait_elite
					trait = katzen_trait_blitzkrieg
					trait = leader_trait_cautious
				}
				effect = {
					save_event_target_as = katzen_admiral
				}
			}
			create_fleet = { #Spawn a big one and 2 small ones
				name = "Unterraumboot Flotte I"
				settings = {
					spawn_debris = no
					can_upgrade = no
					uses_naval_capacity = no
					can_change_composition = no
				}
				effect = {
					set_owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
					while = {
						count = 12 #12 submarines, big pack
						create_ship = {
							name = random
							design = "Kimitz"
							prefix = no
							effect = { set_disable_at_health = 0.05 set_name = "U-Boot" }
						}
					}
					set_fleet_flag = katzen_submarine_fleet
					assign_leader = event_target:katzen_admiral
					set_location = {

				}

					spawn_debris = no
					can_upgrade = no
					uses_naval_capacity = no
					can_change_composition = no
				}
				effect = {
					set_owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country

						count = 6 #6 submarines, small pack
						create_ship = {
							name = random
							design = "Kimitz"
							prefix = no
							effect = { set_disable_at_health = 0.05 set_name = "U-Boot" }
						}
					}
					set_fleet_flag = katzen_submarine_fleet
					assign_leader = event_target:katzen_admiral
					set_location = {
						target = event_target:gigaflusion
						distance = 50
						angle = random
					}
					set_formation_scale = 2
				}
			}
			# create_leader = {
			# 	class = admiral
			# 	species = event_target:flusion_katzens
			# 	name = "Jetstream Katmuel"
			# 	skill = 3
			# 	gender = male

#Submerge test
fleet_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.8503
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_submarine_fleet_ship_count
			value = 0
		}
		ROOT = { #Count submarines
			every_owned_ship = {
				ROOT = {
					change_variable = {
						which = giga_submarine_fleet_ship_count
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		create_fleet = {
			name = "Subspace Disruption"
			settings = {
				spawn_debris = no
				can_upgrade = no
				uses_naval_capacity = no
				can_change_composition = no
				is_boss = yes
			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = event_target:katzen_submarine_country
				while = {
					count = 1 #test
					create_ship = {
						name = random
						design = "Anomalous Subspace"
						prefix = no
					}
				}
				set_fleet_flag = submerged_katzen_submarines_fleet
				set_location = {
					target = ROOT
					distance = 1
					angle = random
				}
				set_fleet_stance = passive
				set_variable = {
					which = giga_submarine_fleet_ship_count
					value = ROOT.giga_submarine_fleet_ship_count
				}
				fleet_event = { id = giga_katzen.8508 days = 360 }
				every_country = {
					set_faction_hostility = {
						target = event_target:katzen_submarine_country
						set_hostile = no
						set_neutral = yes
						set_friendly = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
		delete_fleet = ROOT
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		}
		every_country = {
			set_faction_hostility = {
				target = ROOT
				set_hostile = no
				set_neutral = yes
				set_friendly = no
			}
		}
		set_owner = FROM.owner
	}
}

#unsubmerge test
fleet_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.8505
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		create_fleet = {
			name = "Unterraumboot Flotte"
			settings = {
				spawn_debris = no
				can_upgrade = no
				uses_naval_capacity = no
				can_change_composition = no
			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country
				while = {
					count = ROOT.giga_submarine_fleet_ship_count
					create_ship = {
						name = random
						design = "Kimitz"
						prefix = no
						effect = { set_disable_at_health = 0.05 set_name = "U-Boot" }
					}
				}
				set_location = {
					target = ROOT
					distance = 1
					angle = random
				}
				set_formation_scale = 2
				set_fleet_flag = katzen_submarine_fleet
			}
		}
		delete_fleet = ROOT
	}
}

#ACTUAL EVENTS
#When a Katzen submarine fleets enters the space of a hostile empire, they immediately submerge and locate a planet to head to.
fleet_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.8506
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_fleet_flag = katzen_submarine_fleet
		from = {
			OR = { 
				NOT = { any_system_planet = { is_colony = yes } }
				OR = {
					any_ship_in_system = { is_ship_size = giga_massive_planet }
					any_ship_in_system = { is_ship_size = giga_planet_behemoth }
					any_ship_in_system = { is_ship_size = giga_systemcraft }
				}
			}
			exists = starbase
			starbase = { space_owner = { is_at_war_with = event_target:flusion_primitives_country } }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_submarine_fleet_ship_count
			value = 0
		}
		ROOT = { #Count submarines
			every_owned_ship = {
				ROOT = {
					change_variable = {
						which = giga_submarine_fleet_ship_count
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		create_fleet = {
			name = "Subspace Disruption"
			settings = {
				spawn_debris = no
				can_upgrade = no
				uses_naval_capacity = no
				can_change_composition = no
				is_boss = yes
			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = event_target:katzen_submarine_country
				while = {
					count = 1 #test
					create_ship = {
						name = random
						design = "Anomalous Subspace"
						prefix = no
					}
				}
				set_fleet_flag = submerged_katzen_submarines_fleet
				set_location = {
					target = ROOT
					distance = 1
					angle = random
				}
				set_fleet_stance = passive
				set_variable = {
					which = giga_submarine_fleet_ship_count
					value = ROOT.giga_submarine_fleet_ship_count
				}
				fleet_event = { id = giga_katzen.8508 days = 360 }
				every_country = {
					establish_communications_no_message = event_target:katzen_submarine_country # Don't try to change the hostility unless they know eachother, it does funky shit
					set_faction_hostility = {
						target = event_target:katzen_submarine_country
						set_hostile = no
						set_neutral = yes
						set_friendly = no
					}
				}
				ROOT.from.starbase.owner = {
					random_owned_planet = { 
						limit = { is_colony = yes }
						save_event_target_as = katzen_submarine_target 
					}
				}
				queue_actions = { #Move to a planet (cool!)
					find_closest_system = {
						trigger = {
							id = giga_blokkat.8506.trigger.1
							any_system_planet = { 
								is_planet = event_target:katzen_submarine_target
							}
						}
						found_system = {
							move_to = this
							find_closest_planet = {
								trigger = {
									id = giga_blokkat.8506.trigger.3
									is_planet = event_target:katzen_submarine_target
								}
								found_planet = {
									move_to = this
									orbit_planet = this
								}
							} 
						}
						failed = { #If failed, move to a random planet
							effect = {
								id = giga_blokkat.8506.trigger.5
								queue_actions = { #Move to a planet (cool!)
									find_closest_system = {
										trigger = {
											id = giga_blokkat.8506.trigger.2
											any_system_planet = { owner = { is_country = ROOT.from.starbase.owner } }
										}
										found_system = { 
											move_to = this
											find_closest_planet = {
												trigger = {
													id = giga_blokkat.8506.trigger.4
													is_colony = yes
												}
												found_planet = {
													move_to = this
													orbit_planet = this
												}
											} 
										}
										failed = {
											effect = {
												id = giga_blokkat.8506.trigger.6
												katzen_submarine_unsubmerge = yes
											} 
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		delete_fleet = ROOT
	}
}

#Unsubmerge if:
#The system has a fleet weaker than the submarines
#The system has a planet
fleet_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.8507
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_fleet_flag = submerged_katzen_submarines_fleet
		OR = {
			from = { # Has colony
				exists = starbase
				OR = {
					AND = {
						starbase = { owner = { is_at_war_with = event_target:flusion_primitives_country } }
						any_system_planet = {
							is_colony = yes
							owner = { is_at_war_with = event_target:flusion_primitives_country }
							NOT = { has_orbital_bombardment = yes }
						}
					}
					any_system_planet = {
						is_colony = yes
						owner = { is_at_war_with = event_target:flusion_primitives_country }
						NOT = { has_orbital_bombardment = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			from = {
				OR = {
					any_system_planet = {
						OR = {
							is_planet_class = pc_giga_maginot_world
							is_planet_class = pc_giga_maginot_gas_giant
							has_modifier = maginot_anti_jump_star_modifier
						}
					}
					starbase = { has_starbase_building = katzen_submarine_snare }
				}
			}
			# from = { # Not owned and no hostiles
			# 	NOT = { exists = starbase }
			# 	NOR = {
			# 		any_fleet_in_system = { owner = { is_hostile_to = event_target:flusion_primitives_country } }
			# 		any_fleet_in_system = { owner = { is_at_war_with = event_target:flusion_primitives_country } }
			# 	}
			# }
			# from = {
			# 	exists = starbase
			# 	starbase = { owner = { is_country = event_target:flusion_primitives_country } }
			# }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				solar_system = {
					NOR = {
						any_ship_in_system = { is_ship_size = giga_massive_planet }
						any_ship_in_system = { is_ship_size = giga_planet_behemoth }
						any_ship_in_system = { is_ship_size = giga_systemcraft }
					}
				}
			}
			katzen_submarine_unsubmerge = yes
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					solar_system = {
						NOR = {
							any_system_planet = {
								OR = {
									is_planet_class = pc_giga_maginot_world
									is_planet_class = pc_giga_maginot_gas_giant
									has_modifier = maginot_anti_jump_star_modifier
								}
							}
							starbase = { has_starbase_building = katzen_submarine_snare }
						}
					}
				}
				queue_actions = {
					find_closest_system = {
						trigger = {
							id = giga_blokkat.8507.trigger.1
							any_system_planet = { has_planet_flag = gigaflusion }
						}
						found_system = {
							move_to = this
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				katzen_submarine_unsubmerge = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	}
}

		}
	}
}

###COUNT FOR EVENT CHAIN###
#Count Katzen ships destroyed
country_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.9997

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		fromfrom = {
			OR = {
				is_ship_size = giga_katzen_submarine
				is_ship_size = giga_katzen_bomber
				is_ship_size = giga_katzen_panzer
				is_ship_size = giga_katzen_cruiser
				is_ship_size = giga_kaiser_moon_flusion
			}
		}
		is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
	}

	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
			}
			add_event_chain_counter = {
				event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
				counter = "katzen_ships_lost"
				amount = 1
			}
			add_event_chain_counter = {
				event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
				counter = "katzen_ship_count"
				amount = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#Count ships destroyed by Katzens
country_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.9998

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {

	}

	immediate = {

				has_event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
			}
			add_event_chain_counter = {

				counter = "ships_lost_to_katzen"
				amount = 1
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.9999

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		any_country = {
			is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
			}
			reset_event_chain_counter = { event_chain = katzenartig_chain counter = katzen_ship_count }
			reset_event_chain_counter = { event_chain = katzenartig_chain counter = katzen_planet_count }
			reset_event_chain_counter = { event_chain = katzenartig_chain counter = katzen_warforge_count }
			reset_event_chain_counter = { event_chain = katzenartig_chain counter = katzen_system_count }
		}
		country_event = { id = giga_katzen.9999 days = 30 } #Count again
		every_owned_ship = { #counts ships
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_ship_size = giga_katzen_submarine
					is_ship_size = giga_katzen_bomber
					is_ship_size = giga_katzen_panzer
					is_ship_size = giga_katzen_cruiser
					is_ship_size = giga_kaiser_moon_flusion
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
				}
				add_event_chain_counter = {
					event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
					counter = "katzen_ship_count"
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		every_planet_within_border = { #count planets
			limit = {
				is_colony = yes
				exists = owner
				owner = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
				}
				add_event_chain_counter = {
					event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
					counter = "katzen_planet_count"
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_megastructure = { #count forges
			limit = {
				is_megastructure_type = katzen_forge_1
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
				}
				add_event_chain_counter = {
					event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
					counter = "katzen_warforge_count"
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		every_system_within_border = { #count systems
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
				}
				add_event_chain_counter = {
					event_chain = "katzenartig_chain"
					counter = "katzen_system_count"
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

###KAISER MOON MEGA###
country_event = { #lets reverse engineer the kaiser moon
	id = giga_katzen.0900
	title = "giga_katzen.0900.name"
	desc = "giga_katzen.0900.desc"
	location = from
	is_triggered_only = yes

	picture = GFX_evt_cold_barren
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal

	trigger = {
		event_target:flusion_primitives_country = {
			has_country_flag = kaiser_moon_destroyed
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = katzenartig_improbable }
	}

	option = { #yes
		name = "giga_katzen.0900.a"
		enable_special_project = {
			name = "REPAIR_KAISER_PROJECT"
			location = event_target:kaiser_moon_broken
			owner = root
		}
	}

	option = { #no
		name = "giga_katzen.0900.b"
	}
}

ship_event = {
	id = giga_katzen.0901
	title = "giga_katzen.0901.name"
	desc = "giga_katzen.0901.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_cold_barren
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { 
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = kaiser_moon_tech_possible
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "giga_katzen.0901.a"
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = katzenartig_stellarite
				}
				add_research_option = giga_tech_stellarite_kaiser_moon
				add_tech_progress = {
					tech = giga_tech_stellarite_kaiser_moon
					progress = 0.35
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_research_option = giga_tech_kaiser_moon
				add_tech_progress = {
					tech = giga_tech_kaiser_moon
					progress = 0.35
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

###KAISER CHAIN###
country_event = { #missing kaiser
	id = giga_katzen.0941
	title = "giga_katzen.0941.name"
	desc = "giga_katzen.0941.desc"

	picture = GFX_evt_alien_propaganda
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #what!
		name = "giga_katzen.0941.a"
		enable_special_project = {
			name = "FIND_KAISER_PROJECT"
			location = event_target:gigaflusion

#Conclusion
country_event = { #KAISER IS HERE (text)
	id = giga_katzen.0952
	title = "giga_katzen.0952.name"
	desc = "giga_katzen.0952.desc"

	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	picture = GFX_evt_clocks

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #what!
		name = "giga_katzen.0952.a"
		event_target:gigaflusion = {
			add_deposit = d_flusion_kaiser_rift
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_technology = giga_tech_tetradimensional_engineering }}
				add_research_option = giga_tech_tetradimensional_engineering
				add_tech_progress = {
					tech = giga_tech_tetradimensional_engineering
					progress = 0.25
				}
			}
			add_resource = {
				physics_research = 30000
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				if = {
					limit = { #Achievement
						NOT = {  has_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser7 }
					}
					set_country_flag = giga_achievement_kaiser7
					set_timed_country_flag = { flag = giga_achievement_kaiser7_notification days = 30 }
					giga_achievement_sound = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

###DEBUG###
planet_event = { #spawn debug grandbunny army
	id = giga_katzen.993

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = grandbunny_command_summoner
		}
		create_fleet = { #Spawn some armies
			name = "Grandbunny's Will"
			settings = {
				spawn_debris = no
				can_upgrade = no
				uses_naval_capacity = no
			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = event_target:grandbunny_command_summoner
				while = {
					count = 1
					create_army_transport = {
						army_type = the_grandbunny_debug
						species = event_target:paluush_portrait
					}
				}
				set_location = {
					target = ROOT
					distance = 10
					angle = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

planet_event = {
	id = giga_flusion_terraform.1000

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		has_planet_flag = gigaflusion
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_flusion_gaia_ecu }
				has_modifier = flusion_arcology_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = flusion_arcology_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #solaktropa removed if ocean (duh)
				OR = {
					is_planet_class = pc_ocean
					habitable_planet = no
				}
				OR = {
					has_deposit = d_solaktropa_project
					has_deposit = d_solaktropa_project_wreck
					has_deposit = d_katlantropa_project
					has_deposit = d_katlantropa_project_wreck
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { has_deposit = d_solaktropa_project }
				remove_deposit = d_solaktropa_project
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { has_deposit = d_solaktropa_project_wreck }
				remove_deposit = d_solaktropa_project_wreck
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { has_deposit = d_katlantropa_project }
				remove_deposit = d_katlantropa_project
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { has_deposit = d_katlantropa_project_wreck }
				remove_deposit = d_katlantropa_project_wreck
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_gaia }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_gaia_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_ocean }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_ocean_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_nuked }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_nuked_entity }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } remove_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_katzenland }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_deserted_entity }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } remove_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier }	
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_city }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_city_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_giga_planetary_computer }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_computer_entity} 
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_hive }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_hive_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_machine }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_machine_entity } 
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_plush }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_fluffy_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_ll_foggy }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_foggy_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_ll_temperate }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_lifeless_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_ll_torrid }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_torrid_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_molten }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_molten_entity }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } remove_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier }	
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_shrouded }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_shrouded_entity }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } remove_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_acot_awesome_planet_class = yes }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_acot_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_wet = yes
					is_planet_class = pc_tropical
					is_planet_class = pc_continental 
				}
			}
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_entity }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier }
				} 
				add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } 
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_dry = yes 
					is_planet_class = pc_desert
					is_planet_class = pc_arid
					is_planet_class = pc_savannah
				}
			}
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_desert_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_cold = yes
					giga_is_frozen = yes
					is_planet_class = pc_arctic
					is_planet_class = pc_alpine
				}
			}
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_arctic_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_planet_class = pc_shattered
					is_planet_class = pc_shattered_2
					is_planet_class = pc_broken
					giga_is_barren_cn = yes
					giga_is_frozen = yes
					giga_is_toxic = yes
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } remove_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_planet_class = pc_flusion_gaia_ecu }
			set_planet_entity = { entity = flusion_planet_ecugaia_01_entity }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_rich_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_rich_modifier days = -1 } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_deposit = d_solaktropa_project_wreck }
				remove_deposit = d_solaktropa_project_wreck
				add_deposit = d_solaktropa_project
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_deposit = d_katlantropa_project_wreck }
				remove_deposit = d_katlantropa_project_wreck
				add_deposit = d_katlantropa_project
			}
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = flusion_arcology_modifier } } add_modifier = { modifier = flusion_arcology_modifier days = -1 } }
		}
	}
}
